THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION, CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
(Roc. No. H1/7240/2020)
No.VI(1)/324(b-1)/2020.
Notice under Section 15(1) of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(TN Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land 
Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019) 
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be 
acquired under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Strengthening and 
widening of SH-40, Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram via Palayamkottai Road at KM (11/550 to 12/800) Veeramanickam Village 
in Tiruchendur Taluk, Thoothukudi District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to 
be awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Tirunelveli 
(CKICP), Tamil Nadu after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such 
lands as the case may do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Commissioner of Land Administration (FAC) hereby acquires that the Dry and Wet lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below 
and measuring to an extent of 3108 sq.mts., of lands in Veeramanickam Village in Tiruchendur Taluk, Thoothukudi District, 
to the same, a little more or less needed for Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways 
purpose, to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-40, Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram via Palayamkottai Road at KM 
(11/550 to 12/800). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project in Tirunelveli may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.
No. 383] 
CHENNAI, FRIDAY, SEPTEMBER 18, 2020 
 
 
 
 
 
Purattasi 2, Saarvari, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2051

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
3
(Roc.No.CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH-115/45/2020)
No. VI(1)/324(b-2)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Widening of SH-115, Cheyyur - 
Vandavasi – Polur Road at KM (35/100 to 38/400) 174.salavedu village  in Vandavasi Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District, and 
it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid out of 
the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Vandavasi (CKICP), Tamil Nadu after having considering 
the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish 
the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Wet, Dry and Manai lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to 
an extent of 13727sq.mts. of Wet, Dry and R.Manai lands are acquired in 174.Salavedu village inVandavasi Taluk, 
Tiruvannamalai District, to the same, a little more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project 
for State Highways purpose, to wit for Widening of SH-115, Cheyyur - Vandavasi – Polur Road at KM (35/100 to 38/400). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land 
Acquisition),Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land 
Acquisition), Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Vandavasi in Tiruvannamalai District may be inspected 
at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Tiruvannamalai District, Vandavasi Taluk, 174. Salavedu Village.

mts
(Roc.No. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH 79/46/2020)
No.VI(1)/324(b-3)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired 
under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening of 
SH-79 Tiruchengode to Erode Road at Km 90.600 to 91.100 Km 16.Pallipalayam, Village Kumarapalayam Taluk, Namakkal 
District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be 
paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Salem (CKICP), Tamil Nadu, after having 
considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be, do 
hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 
34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with 
the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the following lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to an extent of 5078 sq.mtrs. 
of Dry lands in 16.Palliplayam, in Kumarapalayam Taluk, Namakkal District, to the same, a little more or less is needed 
for Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, to wit for Strengthening and widening 
of SH-79 Tiruchengode to Erode Road at Km 90.600 to 91.100 Km.
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
– Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tiruchengode, Namakkal District which may be inspected at any time during 
the oﬃ  ce hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired 
under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening of 
SH-79 Tiruchengode to Erode Road at Km 88.200 to 89.070 Km 15.Kadachanallur (Part-II) Village, Kumarapalayam 
Taluk, Namakkal District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Salem (CKICP), Tamil 
Nadu, after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the 
case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and 
Validation) Act, 2019.


 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
19
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read 
with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the following lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to an extent of 4648 
sq.mtrs. of Dry lands in 15.Kadachanallur (Part-II) Village, in Kumarapalayam Taluk, Namakkal District, to the same, a 
little more or less is needed for Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, to wit 
for Strengthening and widening of SH-79 Tiruchengode to Erode Road at Km 88.200 to 89.070 Km.
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
– Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tiruchengode Namakkal District which may be inspected at any time during 
the oﬃ  ce hours.

Total Land Acquisition Area 
4648 sq. mtrs.,
                                                              
(Roc.No. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH 64/48/2020)
No.VI(1)/324(b-5)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired 
under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening of 
SH-64 Kumbakonam – Sirkali Road (From 15/250 K.m to 17/790 K.m) 47. Narasinganpettai Village, Thiruvidaimaruthur 
Taluk, Thanjavur District and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for 
the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Kumbakonam (CKICP), 
Tamil Nadu, after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as 
the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and 
Validation) Act, 2019.


 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
45
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with 
the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the following lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to an extent of 3339 sq.mtrs. 
of Dry, Wet and Manai lands in 47. Narasinganpettai Village, Thiruvidaimaruthur Taluk, Thanjavur District, to the same, 
a little more or less is needed for Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, to wit 
for Strengthening and widening of SH-64 Kumbakonam – Sirkali Road (From 15/250 K.m to 17/790 K.m).
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and oﬃ  ce of the Revenue Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project Kumbakonam which may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce 
hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Strengthening and Widening 
of SH-09 Cuddalore - Madapattu Road at KM 24/900 to KM 26/100 No.29.Thorapadi (Additional) Village in Panruti 
Taluk, Cuddalore District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Cuddalore (CKICP),
Tamil Nadu after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as 
the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
NOTICE

Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Dry lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent 
4038 sq.mt of lands are acquired in No. 29.Thorapadi (Additional) Village in Panruti Taluk, Cuddalore District, to the 
same, a little more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, 
to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-09 Cuddalore-Madapattu Road at KM 24/900 to KM 26/100.

Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project Cuddalore, in Cuddalore District may be inspected at any time during 
the oﬃ  ce hours.

(Roc. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH09/52/2020.)
No.VI(I)/324(b-8)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening 
of SH-09 Cuddalore-Madapattu Road at KM 24/900 to KM 26/100 No.29.Thorapadi Village in Panruti Taluk, Cuddalore 
District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to 
be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Cuddalore (CKICP), Tamilnadu after 
having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may 
be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 
(TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Wet & Dry lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent 
21114 sq.mt of lands are acquired in No.29.Thorapadi Village in Panruti Taluk, Cuddalore District, to the same, a little 
more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, to wit for 
Strengthening and widening of SH-09 Cuddalore-Madapattu  Road at KM 24/900 to KM 26/100 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Cuddalore in Cuddalore District may be inspected at any time during 
the oﬃ  ce hours.

No.VI(I)/324(b-9)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu havingbeen satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired under 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Projectfor Highways purpose for Widening of SH-63, Thanjavur - Mannargudi 
Road at (From K.M of 07/560 to 10/260)12/1.Sadaiyarkovil village in OrathanaduTaluk, Thanjavur District,and it having 
already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds 
controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Kumbakonam (CKICP), Tamil Nadu after having considering the 
cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish 
the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).


 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
83
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of6631sq.mts. 
ofDry, Wet, Manai and Manavari landsare acquired in 12/1.Sadaiyar kovil villagein Orathanadu Taluk, Thanjavur District, 
to the same, a little more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari  Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways 
purpose, for Widening ofSH-63, Thanjavur - Mannargudi Road at (From K.M of 07/560 to 10/260). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land 
Acquisition),Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land 
Acquisition), Chennai –Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project in Kumbakonam which may be inspected at any time 
during the oﬃ  ce hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule 
below are acquired under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose 
to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-23, Mayiladuthurai-Tiruvarur Road at KM (10/400 to 
12/780) Keeranur (Additional) Village in Nannilam Taluk, Tiruvarur District, and it having already 
been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid 
out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Kumbakonam (CKICP),
Tamil Nadu after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest 
on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) 
of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 
34 of 2002) the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Wet lands speciﬁ ed in the 
schedule below and measuring to an extent of 131 sq.mts of Wet and Manai lands are acquired 
in Keeranur (Additional) Village in Nannilam Taluk, Tiruvarur District, to the same, a little more or 
less is needed for Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, 
to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-23, Mayiladuthurai-Tiruvarur Road at KM (10/400 to 
12/780). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue 
oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and 
oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor 
Project, Tiruvarur which may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.

Notice under Section 15(1) of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001(TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land 
Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Strengthening and widening 
of SH-23, Mayiladuthurai - Thiruvarur Road (From K.M of 6/100 to 7/500 K.M) 21.Pandaravadai Village, Kuttalam Taluk, 
Nagapattinam District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer, (Highways) Chennai – Kanyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having 
interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws(Revival 
of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), read 
with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Wet, Dry and Manai lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an 
extent of 5507 sq.mt of lands are acquired in 21.Pandaravadai Village in Kuttalam Taluk, Nagapattinam District, to the 
same, a little more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, 
to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-23, Mayiladuthurai - Thiruvarur Road (From K.M of 6/100 to 7/500 K.M).
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Sirkali which may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(Roc.No. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH64/56/2020)
No.VI(I)/324(b-12)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Strengthening and widening 
of SH-64, Kumbakonam - Sirkali Road at KM (9/280 to 11/360) 61.Mahathanapuram Village in Thiruvidaimaruthur Taluk, 
Thanjavur District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for 
the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Kumbakonam (CKICP),
Tamil Nadu after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest on such lands as 
the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Dry, Wet and Manai lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an 
extent of 667 sq.mt of lands are acquired in 61.Mahathanapuram Village in Thiruvidaimaruthur Taluk, Thanjavur District, 
to the same, a little more or less is needed for Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways 
purpose, to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-64, Kumbakonam - Sirkali Road at KM (9/280 to 11/360). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Thanjavur  District, Thiruvidaimaruthur Taluk, 61. MahathanapuramVillage

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
103
(Roc.No. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH66/58/2020)
No.VI(I)/324(b-13)/2020.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for Strengthening and widening 
of SH-66, Kumbakonam - Mannarkudi Road (From K.M of 6/400 to 8/300 K.M) Thippirajapuram Village, Kumbakonam 
Taluk, Thanjavur District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer, (Highways) Chennai – 
Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons having 
interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws(Revival 
of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), read 
with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby notify that the Wet, Dry and Manai lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an 
extent of 4665 sq.mt of lands are acquired in Thippirajapuram Village in Kumbakonam Taluk, Thanjavur District, to the 
same, a little more or less needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, 
to wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-66, Kumbakonam - Mannarkudi Road (From K.M of 6/400 to 8/300 K.M).
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam may be inspected at any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.

Total Land Acquisition Area :
4665  Sq. mtrs.,
Roc. CKICP/CLA/15(1)/SH23/59/2020
No. VI(1)/324(b-14)/2020
The Government of Tamil Nadu having  been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project  for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening 
of SH-23 Mayiladuthurai - Thiruvarur Road at Km 15/400 to Km 16/850 Peralam Village in Nannilam Taluk, Thiruvarur 
District,  and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to 
be paid out of the funds  controlled and  managed by the Divisional Engineer, Kumbakonam, (CKICP), Tamil Nadu 
after having considered the cause shown by the owner or other persons having interest in the said lands, as the case 
may be do hereby published the following notice under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 
2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).


 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
117
NOTICE
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to an extent 345 of 
sq.mt of Wet lands in  Peralam Village in Nannilam Taluk, Thiruvarur District, to be the same, a little more or less is 
needed for Chennai – Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project  for Highways purpose, to wit, for strengthening and 
widening of  SH-23 Mayiladuthurai - Thiruvarur Road at Km 15/400 to Km 16/850.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are acquired 
under Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for Highways purpose to wit for strengthening and widening 
of SH-58-2, Kancheepuram – Arakkonam – Tiruttani Road from KM 97/250 to KM 98/200 No.63.Melpakkam (Part-
2) (Additional) village, Arakkonam Taluk, Ranipet District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional 


118 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
Engineer(H), Kancheepuram (CKICP), Tamil Nadu after having considering the cause shown by the owner or other 
persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-
section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land 
Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act,2019.
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with 
the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019, the Governor of Tamil 
Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the Dry lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent 120 of sq.mt of 
lands are acquired in No.63.Melpakkam (Part-2) (Additional) village, Arakkonam  Taluk, Ranipet District, to the same, a 
little more or less is needed for Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project for State Highways purpose, to wit 
for Strengthening and widening of SH-58-2, Kancheepuram – Arakkonam –Tiruttani Road from  KM 97/250 to KM 98/200.
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the Special District Revenue oﬃ  cer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project Arakkonamin Ranipet District may be inspected at any time during 
the oﬃ  ce hours.
